# Course Input Data

# Game Concept / GDD
# **1. Core Fantasy**

Sigilborne is a **lifelong ninja-life simulator** inside a fully simulated magical world.

The player starts as a young, inexperienced ninja who:
- learns hand-signs (glyphs)    
- discovers techniques through teachers, scrolls, practice    
- trains like Naruto learning the Rasengan    
- explores a living world that changes without them    
- pursues mastery across decades of in-world time    
- can become a legendary figure feared, hunted, revered, or mythologized    

Every world is unique.  
Every life is unique.  
Every technique is earned.

Sigilborne captures the exact emotional journey of:
- early clumsy chakra control    
- intense practice and discipline    
- discovering or inventing jutsu    
- improving combos    
- achieving fluid mastery    
- eventually becoming someone the world must react to    

---

# **2. Core Loop**

### **Early Game**

You are weak, untrained, unsure.  
Learn basic glyphs â†’ practice â†’ improve â†’ slowly decipher the worldâ€™s magical logic.

### **Mid Game**

You gain stable techniques, join or oppose clans, explore ruins, train with teachers, and become a meaningful ninja in the world.

### **Late Game**

You are a master of certain categories of magic.  
Enemies fear you.  
Factions react to your presence.  
Forbidden arts become accessible.  
You shape the world.

### **Generational Continuity**

If your character dies:

- you return to the main menu    
- the **world persists**    
- your legend remains    
- a new character may enter the same world and discover your legacy    

This creates multi-life sagas inside a single living world.

---

# **3. World Identity**

Each world is a fully simulated magical ecosystem with:

- procedural clans    
- dynamically evolving settlements    
- NPC literacy distributions    
- biome resonance    
- anomalies and forbidden zones    
- unique glyph â†’ category â†’ subtype mappings    
- a unique magical history and â€œeraâ€
- evolving political states and conflicts    

The world exists **with or without the player**.

NPCs learn, mutate, form factions, form clans, rebel, die, remember, and mythologize.

---

# **4. Glyph System (High-Level)**

### **Glyphs are hand-signs â€” the universal language of ninjutsu.**

- Every world uses ~50â€“80 glyphs drawn from a large global pool.    
- Each glyph has:    
    - its **symbol** (the sign)        
    - its **mechanical category** (stable)        
    - its **subtype** (world-specific meaning)        

Players learn glyphs through:
- teachers    
- observation    
- scrolls    
- ruins    
- anomalies    
- experimentation    
- bloodline resonance

Solo casting reveals hints.
Combining glyphs creates techniques.
Mastery creates shortcuts.
Forbidden interactions create forbidden jutsu.

---

# **5. Combo & Spell System (High-Level)**

Combos are **freeform**:
- any sequence can be attempted    
- the worldâ€™s logic interprets them    
- new combos emerge each world    
- NPCs, clans, and cultures have their own combos    

Low mastery â†’ unstable.  
Medium mastery â†’ reliable.  
High mastery â†’ fluid and expressive.  
Legendary mastery â†’ mythic power.

Combo discovery is core to the playerâ€™s identity.

---

# **6. Chakra Stability & Chaos Residue (High-Level)**

The playerâ€™s chakra is:
- unstable early    
- controllable mid    
- refined late    

Casting causes instability.  
Failure causes chaos residue.  
Chaos residue:
- mutates    
- destabilizes    
- enhances forbidden paths    
- increases risk    
- increases reward    

This system fuels the tension of powerful ninjutsu.

---

# **7. Bloodlines**

Each world generates unique variants of stable bloodline templates.

Bloodlines awaken through:
- trauma    
- stress    
- near-death    
- resonance    
- narrative events    

Bloodlines evolve into:
- adaptive paths    
- volatile paths    
- corruptive paths    
- ascendant paths    

Bloodlines help the player break limits.

---

# **8. Clans, Settlements, Social Structures**

Clans are **semi-stable archetypes** (Martial, Scholar, Spirit, Assassin, etc.)  
Each world generates procedural variants:
- names    
- symbols    
- histories    
- bloodline ties    
- forbidden secrets    

Clans can form dynamically (e.g., Akatsuki-like rogue groups).

Settlements evolve:
- politically    
- socially    
- magically    
- economically    
- through conflict and corruption    
- reactively to the player    

NPC memory spans generations.

---

# **9. Combat**

Combat is tactical, positioning-based, and timing-sensitive.

It combines:
- hand-sign casting    
- chakra enhancement    
- martial arts    
- weapons    
- stealth    
- mobility    

Enemies and NPCs follow the same system.

Combat difficulty scales with ambition:
- stealth might save your life    
- direct confrontation might end it    

---

# **10. Death & Legacy**

Death ends the character, **not the world**.

Your actions become:
- stories    
- myths    
- journal entries    
- ruin inscriptions    
- clan gossip    
- environmental scars    

A new character can enter the same world and interact with your former legacy.

This creates emergent multi-life narratives.
_Core subsystem of Sigilborne â€” the universal language of ninjutsu._

---

# **1. What a Glyph Is**

A **glyph** is a _hand-sign symbol_ â€” a discrete, learnable unit of ninjutsu.  
Every glyph has three layers:

### **Layer 1 â€” Symbol (Visual Hand-Sign)**

- The actual in-game hand gesture.    
- Unique symbol across the global database.    
- Players recognize and map them to hotbar slots.    
- NPCs use the same signs.    

### **Layer 2 â€” Mechanical Category (Stable Across All Worlds)**

This is the glyphâ€™s **fundamental magical archetype**.

Examples (not final, but aligned):
- Bloom (growth, expansion)    
- Veil (concealment, distortion)    
- Pulse (shock, bursts)    
- Bind (control, restraint)    
- Consume (drain, corruption)    
- Fracture (division, instability)    
- Echo (duplication, resonance)    
- Project (beams, projectiles)    
- Conjure (materialization)    
- Shape (form manipulation)    
- Flux (transformation)    
- Chain (propagation)    

**Categories never change** â€” this gives long-term player intuition.

### **Layer 3 â€” Subtype (World-Specific Behavior)**

Each glyphâ€™s actual effect â€” its â€œmeaningâ€ â€” is generated uniquely per world.

Examples:
- Bloom might mean _toxic bloom_ in one world    
- or _healing growth_ in another    
- or _spore cloud_ in a swamp biome    

Subtypes depend on:
- world history    
- biomes    
- anomalies    
- clan traditions    
- ancient ruins    
- magical density    
- chaos residue conditions    

This is what guarantees infinite replayability.

---

# **2. Global Glyph Pool**

Sigilborne maintains a **large global database** of hand-sign glyphs (100+ symbols).

### Every world draws **50â€“80** glyphs from this pool

based on:
- world theme    
- history    
- biome distribution    
- anomalies    
- clan literacy    
- forbidden arts    
- NPC cultural development    

This ensures:
- every world feels like a **coherent language**    
- players donâ€™t memorize symbols across worlds    
- but symbols remain _recognizable_ within a world    
- clans, teachers, and scrolls all speak this worldâ€™s â€œdialectâ€    

---

# **3. Player Glyph Repertoire**

A player does **not** learn all 50â€“80 glyphs.

They typically learn:
- **8â€“12 glyphs** early game    
- **12â€“20 glyphs** mid game    
- **20â€“30 glyphs** late game (if they go deep)    

Why?
- naruto-like specialization    
- personal identity    
- replayability    
- mastery focus    
- each life is unique    
- different characters discover different techniques    

You are not meant to know everything.  
You are meant to **discover your own path.**

---

# **4. Glyph Acquisition**

Players learn glyphs through:

### **A) NPC Teachers**
- structured teaching (if in school or clan)    
- informal teaching (if relationships built)    
- demonstrations during missions    
- rituals, meditation, sparring    

Teachers give:
- the sign    
- rough idea of category    
- sometimes a weak demonstration    

But **not the full meaning**.

NPCs may teach incorrect lore if their culture misinterpreted the glyph.

---

### **B) Scrolls & Fragments**
- show hand-sign diagrams    
- show partial combo sequences    
- show misinterpreted lore    
- may contain forbidden variants    
- often incomplete    
- discovered in ruins, enemy camps, ancient temples, etc.    

Scrolls never explain categories literally â€” players interpret them.

---

### **C) Observation**

You see an NPC use the sign â†’ you unlock the **symbol**.  
But to learn it, you must:

- execute it yourself    
- stabilize it through practice    

---

### **D) Solo-Cast Discovery**

You can attempt random signs or combos.  
Highly unstable early game.  
Huge residue risk.  
But possible.

Mirrors Narutoâ€™s tendency to experiment with random signs.

---

### **E) Bloodline Resonance**

Some glyphs â€œcallâ€ to certain bloodlines.  
These signs feel naturally intuitive to the player.  
Early hint toward personal destiny.

---

### **F) Anomaly Revelation**

Chaos anomalies sometimes reveal glyphs directly:
- flicker visions    
- incomplete signs    
- corrupted variants    
- unstable flashes    

Dangerous but powerful discovery path.

---

# **5. Solo-Cast Behavior**

Solo-casting a glyph produces a **weak version** of its subtype.  
Solo-casts are the main way players decipher category meaning.

### Early Game

- unstable    
- flickery    
- misfires    
- strain spikes    
- residue buildup    
- â€œI have no idea what this does yetâ€    

### Mid Game

- readable    
- consistent    
- safe testing possible    

### Late Game

- fluid    
- expressive    
- used as part of big chains    

This mimics:

- Narutoâ€™s early Rasengan failures    
- Wind Chakra training    
- Chakra control practice    

And it strengthens the mastery fantasy.

---

# **6. Glyph Stability (Per-Glyph Skill)**

Each glyph has a **Stability Rating**:
- Low â†’ shaky, unreliable    
- Medium â†’ stable    
- High â†’ mastery â†’ supports shortcuts    

Increasing stability requires:
- repeating solo-casts    
- practicing combos    
- meditating    
- training in resonant biomes    
- sparring    
- teacher discipline sessions    

The more stable a glyph is, the:
- faster the sign appears    
- less strain it causes    
- lower the misfire chance    
- more combos it enables    
- smoother the casting feels    

This forms the backbone of long-term progression.

---

# **7. Category Resonance**

Categories interact with the environment.

Examples:
- Bloom stabilizes faster in forests    
- Consume amplifies in corrupted lands    
- Pulse is unstable in marshes    
- Flux is chaotic near anomalies    
- Veil sharpens in fog or nighttime    

Players learn category identity through:
- solo-casts    
- observations    
- environmental cues    

But **never through explicit UI labels**.

This preserves mystery.

---

# **8. World Mapping Logic**

When generating a world, the game:
1. Selects **50â€“80 glyphs** from the global pool.    
2. Assigns each glyph to a **stable mechanical category** (Bloom, Veil, etc.).    
3. Generates a **single, world-wide subtype** for each glyph based on:    
    - overall world theme        
    - distribution of biomes (but only as input at generation time)        
    - anomaly density and types        
    - major historical events (catastrophes, empires, collapses)        
    - presence and nature of key ruins / temples / spirit sites    
4. Stores this as the **global glyph â†’ category â†’ subtype table** for that world.    
5. Distributes glyph knowledge to NPCs, scrolls, clans, ruins, anomalies, etc.    

> **Rule:** Once generated, a glyphâ€™s subtype is the same everywhere in the world, for everyone.

### **Environmental Resonance (separate from mapping)**

Biomes and locations then **modulate how that fixed subtype behaves**:
- Forests might **stabilize** Bloom but **dampen** Pulse.    
- Volcanic areas might **amplify** Fire-ish Projects but **raise strain**.    
- Marshes might **corrupt** Blooms (more residue buildup, more toxic side effects).    

This changes:
- potency    
- strain    
- stability    
- side effects    

â€¦but **never** the underlying subtype mapping.

---

# **9. Glyph Interaction Rules (High-Level)**

Glyphs interact based on:
- category relationships    
- subtype variations    
- order in sequence    
- stability    
- strain    
- residue    
- environmental resonance    
- userâ€™s bloodline    

Example interactions:
- Bloom â†’ Pulse expands pulse outward    
- Pulse â†’ Bloom compresses bloom into a tight sphere    
- Consume â†’ Conjure creates tainted summons    
- Veil â†’ Project creates invisible projectiles    
- Echo â†’ Pulse creates ripple shockwaves    

These vary by world via subtypes.

---

# **10. Forbidden Glyphs**

Some glyphs are:
- too unstable    
- too dangerous    
- corrupted by the Shattering    
- connected to ancient catastrophes    

Forbidden glyphs:
- cannot be used safely    
- distort symbols    
- shift appearance when stability drops    
- are tied to forbidden arts    

Players should FEEL dread when learning one.

NPCs react strongly:
- fear    
- respect    
- mythology    
- hostility    

---

# **11. Glyph Loss / Corruption**

Glyphs can be lost or corrupted due to:
- death    
- high residue    
- forbidden miscasts    
- bloodline mutations    
- using forbidden zones    
- extreme instability    

Corrupted glyphs twist category logic and change combo behavior.

---

# **12. Glyph UI/UX (High Level)**

- Symbols appear briefly near hands when casting    
- Subtle visual cues hint at category    
- No explicit category names are ever shown    
- Journal sketches glyphs as the player interprets them    
- Misfires cause static/distortion    
- Stability increases clean up the visuals    

This is a â€œdiegetic spell notebookâ€ like Narutoâ€™s jutsu scrolls.

# **1. Overview**

In Sigilborne, **combos** are the core of ninjutsu:  
sequences of hand-sign glyphs executed in order to shape chakra into a technique.

Combos are:
- **freeform** (any sequence can be attempted)    
- **interpreted by world-specific logic**    
- **unstable early, expressive late**    
- **consistent within a world**    
- **discoverable through practice, observation, and experimentation**    

A combo is not a predefined â€œspell.â€  
It is an **emergent behavior** produced by the interaction of:
- glyph categories    
- glyph subtypes    
- sequence order    
- chakra stability    
- strain    
- residue    
- environment    
- bloodline resonance    
- world historical rules    

This system supports the fantasy of:
- Naruto discovering new techniques    
- training arcs    
- signature jutsu    
- forbidden variants    
- clan-specific traditions    
- personal invention    

---

# **2. The Combo Interpreter (Core Mechanic)**

When a player inputs a sequence of glyphs, the gameâ€™s **Combo Interpreter** analyzes the entire chain.

It evaluates:

### **(1) Sequence Order**

(A â†’ B â†’ C is not C â†’ B â†’ A)  
Order defines meaning.

### **(2) Categories**

Each glyph belongs to one of the gameâ€™s **stable universal categories**.  
Categories provide **the grammatical structure** of the magic system.

### **(3) Subtypes (World-Specific Meanings)**

Each glyph has a subtype unique to this world.  
Subtypes provide **the flavor and nuance** of the combo.

### **(4) Stability**

Per-glyph mastery determines how reliably the glyph channels chakra.

### **(5) Strain**

Chakra cost and body stress of maintaining the chain.

### **(6) Residue**

Chaos accumulation affecting risk and corruption.

### **(7) Environment**

Biome resonance, anomalies, weather, day/night.

### **(8) Bloodline Resonance**

Some combos synergize or conflict with your lineage.

### **(9) NPC Cultural Influence**

If this combo is common in a clan, or taboo, or forbidden.

The Interpreter then produces:
- **Full Technique**    
- **Partial Technique**    
- **Fizzle**    
- **Miscast**    
- **Forbidden Surge** (rare, devastating)    

This system allows **infinite techniques** without scripting them manually.

---

# **3. Combo Length Tiers**

Different combo lengths represent different levels of mastery and danger.

### **Tier 1 â€” Single-Glyph Techniques (Solo-Casts)**
- Weak but reliable    
- Used for testing subtypes    
- Foundation of learning a worldâ€™s magic language    

### **Tier 2 â€” 2â€“3 Glyph Combos (Common Jutsu)**
- Core techniques for most ninja    
- Trainable    
- Teachable    
- Often clan-standard techniques    
- Stable by mid-game    

### **Tier 3 â€” 4â€“5 Glyph Combos (Advanced Techniques)**
- Require discipline and timing    
- High power    
- Hard in early game, rewarding mid-game    
- Often associated with elite ninja or teachers    
- Signature moves emerge here    

### **Tier 4 â€” 6â€“7+ Glyph Combos (Elite / Legendary / Forbidden)**
- Rare    
- Dangerous    
- Require extreme stability    
- Heavy residue if miscast    
- May require bloodline resonance    
- Often world-unique legendary techniques    

Only a handful of NPCs â€” or the player â€” will ever master these.

---

# **4. Combo Formation Rules**

### **Rule 1 â€” Any Sequence Can Be Attempted**

There are no invalid inputs.  
Even nonsensical sequences produce _something_:
- a fizzle    
- a faint chakra puff    
- a distorted fragment    
- or a dangerous miscast    

This supports experimentation and discovery.

### **Rule 2 â€” Order Matters**

Same glyphs, different order = different effect.  
Mirrors Narutoâ€™s hand sign semantics.

### **Rule 3 â€” Repetition Matters**

(A â†’ A â†’ B) â‰  (A â†’ B â†’ B)

Repetition:
- reinforces subtype traits    
- increases strain    
- changes stability checks    
- modifies outcome    

### **Rule 4 â€” Categories Define Structure**

Categories create the **core behavior** of combos.

Example:
- Bloom â†’ Veil = â€œexpand + concealâ€    
- Veil â†’ Bloom = â€œconceal + growth burstâ€    

Always consistent _within a world_.

### **Rule 5 â€” Subtypes Define Nuance**

Subtypes give the technique its **color**, e.g.:

Bloom (Spore Bloom) â†’ Veil (Heat Mirage)  
= _expanding shimmering spore-mist that bends light_

Another world:  
Bloom (Healing Bloom) â†’ Veil (Cold Mist Veil)  
= _expanding cold fog that dulls senses and soothes wounds_

Same structure, different flavor.

---

# **5. Technique Outcomes**

### **Full Success**
- clean execution    
- stable chakra flow    
- predictable result    
- low residue    
- occurs at medium â†’ late mastery    

### **Partial Success (Hybrid Mastery Model)**
- early game: often fizzles    
- mid game: weak or distorted versions    
- late game: near-success    

Examples:
- projectile wobbles    
- clone fades quickly    
- range is shorter    
- effect flickers    
- aura is unstable    

Partial success is core to the training fantasy.

### **Fizzle**
- chakra fails to form    
- no real effect    
- low residue    
- light strain  
    Typical early-game result.    

### **Miscast**
- chaotic burst    
- recoil damage    
- area distortion    
- high residue    
- risk of forbidden ripple    
- NPC attention  
    Miscasts create danger and story moments.    

### **Forbidden Surge (Rare)**

Extreme instability causes:
- glyph corruption    
- environmental scars    
- bloodline mutation triggers    
- lethal damage    
- or catastrophic effects    

True forbidden jutsu emerge from these events.

---

# **6. Discovery Through Repetition**

Players naturally improve combos by trying them repeatedly.

Each repetition:
- increases stability    
- reduces fizzle chance    
- unlocks cleaner chakra flow    
- tightens timing windows    
- yields more reliable outcomes    
- advances toward mastery    
- records in the journal    

Eventually, combos become:
- crisp    
- fast    
- clean    
- fluid in combat    

This supports a full Naruto-style training arc.

---

# **7. NPC Combo Literacy**

NPCs use the exact same system as the player.

### NPC tiers:

**Novices:**
- solo-casts    
- simple 2-glyph sequences    
- weak stability    

**Skilled ninja:**
- 2â€“4 glyph combos    
- clan techniques    
- stable execution    

**Elite ninja:**
- 4â€“5 glyph chains    
- strong subtype synergy    
- sharp timing    

**Legends / Sages / Forbidden Practitioners:**
- 6â€“7+ glyph combos    
- shortcut glyphs    
- bloodline-enhanced jutsu    
- forbidden variants    

NPC literacy evolves over the worldâ€™s timeline.

---

# **8. Teacher Techniques**

Teachers teach **sequences**, not spells.

A teacher might show:
- the order    
- the rhythm    
- the intended effect    

But the player must:
- develop stability    
- practice timing    
- refine the combo    
- understand the subtype interactions    
- unlock mastery    

Teacher-taught techniques become **cultural knowledge**.

Players cannot rename these.

---

# **9. Player-Invented Techniques**

Players may _name_ techniques only when:
- the combo sequence is not culturally known    
- no NPC taught it    
- no scroll describes it    
- it is a variant the player personally developed    
- OR it is discovered accidentally    

These become the playerâ€™s **signature jutsu**, recorded in the journal.

NPCs may learn them if:
- they observe the player    
- defeat the player    
- find written notes    
- study the playerâ€™s corpse    

This supports emergent legacy.

---

# **10. Combo Evolution (Late-Game Depth)**

A combo can evolve due to:

### **A) Mastery**

Long sequences may compress into **shortcut sequences** over time.

### **B) Residue**

Heavy residue use may distort techniques into corrupted forms.

### **C) Bloodline Awakening**

Some sequences gain new branches or effects.

### **D) Forbidden Exposure**

Contact with forbidden zones mutates behavior.

### **E) World Events**

Large-scale magical events shift interactions subtly.

This gives combos lifecycles across decades of play.

---

# **11. Legendary Techniques**

A technique becomes legendary when it meets multiple conditions:
- long sequence    
- extreme stability requirement    
- bloodline resonance    
- world-specific forbidden interactions    
- nearly impossible timing    
- world-level danger    
- massive power    
- strong narrative myth    
- mastery by only 1â€“3 beings in history    

Legendary techniques define the worldâ€™s magical identity.

---

# **12. Combo Journal**

The journal records:
- every attempted sequence    
- success / partial / fail tags    
- player annotations    
- teacher demonstrations    
- diagrams    
- observed NPC sequences    

Filtering allows reviewing:
- successful sequences    
- unstable sequences    
- forbidden warnings    
- player-invented jutsu    

This becomes the playerâ€™s research notebook and legacy artifact.

# â­ **B2 Summary**

The Combo System in Sigilborne is:
- freeform but internally logical    
- dangerous early, expressive late    
- world-specific and culturally shaped    
- discoverable through training    
- supports unique player jutsu invention    
- NPC-driven and evolving

_The energetic systems that govern casting difficulty, mastery progression, danger, corruption, and forbidden evolution._

---

# **1. Overview**

Chakra Stability and Chaos Residue form the **core tension** of Sigilborneâ€™s ninjutsu.  
Together they determine:
- how difficult casting is    
- how dangerous long sequences become    
- how mastery emerges    
- how corruption spreads    
- how forbidden techniques evolve    
- how NPCs perceive powerful ninja    
- how worlds change across generations    

Chakra is **life force shaped by discipline**.  
Residue is **chaos accumulated from instability, miscasts, and overexertion**.

This system supports:
- early-game fragility    
- mid-game competence    
- late-game flow-state mastery    
- endgame corruption paths    
- deep world interactivity    
- Naruto-style exhaustion and breakthroughs    

---

# **2. Chakra Strain System**

Chakra strain represents how much stress the ninjaâ€™s body and network endure while channeling signs and combos.

### **Strain Accumulation Model (C + D)**

Strain increases from:

#### **1. Per-Glyph Strain**

Each sign adds incremental load.

- Light categories (Veil, Echo) cost less    
- Heavy categories (Consume, Flux) cost more    
- Neutral categories vary based on subtype    
- Bloodline synergy can reduce cost    
- Bloodline mismatch can increase cost    

#### **2. Per-Technique Final Spike**

When a combo completes, the technique imposes a large strain spike proportional to:

- combo length    
- category interactions    
- subtype synergy    
- cast stability    
- player experience    
- environment resonance    
- residue level    

This creates a system where longer or unstable combos inherently â€œburnâ€ more chakra.

---

# **3. High Strain Consequences**

When strain exceeds safe thresholds, the following occur **in order** depending on severity:

### **A) Physical Fatigue**

- movement slows    
- dodges become sluggish    

### **B) Sensory Distortion**

- blurry vision    
- jittering peripheral effects    
- increased breathing audio    
- flickering hand-sign visuals    

### **C) Technique Unreliability**

- sign recognition windows shrink    
- fizzle chance increases    
- partial success becomes common    
- combo sequencing becomes harder    

### **D) Burnout Events (Collapses)**

When strain passes a dangerous threshold:
- player collapses    
- chakra network shuts down    
- forced recovery window    
- enemies may detect or exploit vulnerability    

### **E) Chakra Regeneration Failure**

At very high strain:
- chakra does not regenerate    
- casting becomes impossible until reset    
- this mirrors heavy Naruto exhaustion    

### **F) Heightened Detection**

Overexerted chakra emits:
- heat    
- light    
- aura    
- spiritual noise    

Enemies become more alert.

### **G) Bloodline Reactions**

Extreme strain can:
- trigger awakenings    
- cause mutations    
- unlock hidden traits    
- push the player toward dangerous evolution paths    

The system intentionally supports â€œbreakthrough under extreme pressure.â€

---

# **4. Strain Reset Mechanisms**

Chakra strain drains only through **deliberate recovery**, reinforcing the ninja-life sim.

Reset methods:

### **B) Natural Recovery (Very Slow)**

- passive    
- takes a long time      

### **C) Meditation**

- fastest safe reset    
- improves with training    
- requires safe space    

### **D) Food / Rest / Sleep**

Just like Narutoâ€™s world:
- food restores chakra faster    
- sleep fully resets strain    
- resting at home, inns, or allies is most efficient    

### **E) Sacred / Resonant Locations**

Shrines, ancient springs, spiritual groves:
- cleanse strain    
- stabilize chakra    
- sometimes reveal glyph insights    
- safe zones for training    

This ties recovery into world exploration.

---

# **5. Chakra Pool Growth Over Lifespan**

Chakra capacity is **not static**.

It grows with:
- age    
- daily training    
- meditation quality    
- clan techniques    
- bloodline awakening    
- major narrative breakthroughs    
- forbidden arts (dangerous)    

This ensures:

- **early game = extremely limited chakra**    
- **mid game = sufficient but risky**    
- **late game = fluid mastery**    

Players become meaningfully stronger over their characterâ€™s lifetime.

---

# **6. Sensory-Driven Representation**

Chakra strain is communicated **purely through sensory feedback**:
- chakra aura weakens    
- signs flicker or shake    
- screen depth-of-field shifts    
- muffled audio under exhaustion    

No explicit UI bars.  
This keeps the experience immersive and matches Narutoâ€™s visual language.

---

# **7. Chaos Residue System**

Residue is the **shadow of chakra**, accumulated from:
- miscasts    
- partial successes    
- long combos    
- unstable subtypes    
- casting near anomalies    
- using forbidden sequences    
- overexertion    

Residue represents both:
- **corruption** (impurity in the chakra network)    
- **dangerous potential** (unstable power that fuels forbidden jutsu)    

This duality is central to late-game depth.

---

# **8. Residue Distribution (Model E)**

Residue accumulates in two places:

### **Player Residue**

- affects clarity    
- increases instability    
- unlocks forbidden paths    
- accelerates bloodline changes    
- increases risk of miscasts    

### **World Residue**

Casting ninjutsu affects the world itself:
- residue bleeds into terrain    
- corrupts wildlife    
- warps local resonance    
- creates temporary anomalies    

World residue:

- **does decay** naturally (slowly)    
- but repeated use can create stable scars    

This ensures long-lived worlds evolve through generations of ninjutsu activity without becoming unplayably corrupted.

---

# **9. Effects of Residue on the World**

Residue has wide-reaching consequences:

### **A) Biome Distortion**

Forests rot, marshes intensify, deserts crack with unstable energy.

### **B) Local Glyph Resonance Shifts**

Some glyphs become more potent or unstable in residue-heavy zones.

### **C) New Anomalies Form**

Tear-like distortions, chakra storms, echoing spirits.

### **D) Wildlife Corruption**

Amplified aggression, mutations, chakra-infused creatures.

### **E) Forbidden Entities Attracted**

Corrupted spirits, ancient echoes, world predators.

### **F) NPC Behavioral Shifts**

Villagers fear residue-heavy zones.  
Forbidden practitioners seek them.

### **G) Forbidden Jutsu Unlocks**

Some techniques are only possible in residue-rich conditions.

### **H) World Scars**

Ruins of past battles remain.  
Future characters can revisit them.

### **I) Magical Weather**

Chakra rain, distortion fog, shimmering storms.

---

# **10. Residue Reversibility**

The player can reverse (or embrace) corruption.

### **B) Meditation / Purification**

- slow    
- safe    
- requires discipline    

### **C) Special Rituals / Quests**

- temples    
- spirit guides    
- ancient techniques    
- rare materials    

### **E) Controlled Corruption Path**

Players can stabilize corruption instead of removing it:
- turning residue into a unique power source    
- unlocking forbidden evolutions    
- becoming a â€œtainted sageâ€ type archetype    

This path is risky and alters NPC perception.

---

# **11. Casting Under High Residue**

When casting with high residue:

### **A) Miscast Chance Rises**

The chakra network is unstable.

### **B) Subtype Mutations**

Spore Bloom â†’ toxic spores â†’ necrotic spores  
Heat Veil â†’ shimmer â†’ mirage â†’ searing mirage

### **C) Technique Outcomes Warp**

Targeting becomes inconsistent.  
Effects grow unpredictable.

### **D) Stability Drops**

Long chains break easily.

### **E) Forbidden Branches Unlock**

Some combos gain new effects if residue is sufficiently high.

### **F) Power Increases (Dangerously)**

Damage, range, intensity spike.

### **G) Sensory Distortion**

Player perception warps.

### **J) NPC Reaction Changes**

Fear, hostility, religious reverence, avoidance.

Residue is not a poison; it is **chaotic potential**.

---

# â­ **B3 Summary**

Chakra Stability & Chaos Residue form a unified system where:
- every glyph stresses the body    
- mastery reduces instability    
- residue reflects the consequences of failure and overreach    
- the world itself reacts to chaos    
- forbidden paths emerge naturally    
- chakra grows with training and age    
- late-game power comes with real risk    
- NPCs respond to your instability    
- worlds evolve across generations    

This is the spiritual and mechanical backbone of ninjutsu in Sigilborne.

_How ninja grow from shaky beginners into fluid, terrifying masters â€” and how long sequences collapse into legendary, near-instant jutsu._

---

# **1. Overview**

Mastery is the backbone of Sigilborneâ€™s ninjutsu.

The player begins with:

- unstable signs    
- frequent miscasts    
- shallow chakra control    

Through decades of training, repetition, and experience, they reach:

- stable execution    
- fluid combo rhythms    
- reduced strain    
- near-instant casting via shortcut glyphs    
- signature techniques    
- bloodline evolutions    
- forbidden forms    

Mastery in Sigilborne follows a **hybrid curve**:

- **Early game:** slow, fragile    
- **Mid game:** steady and meaningful growth    
- **Late game:** fluid, expressive, powerful    
- **Legend tier:** transformative evolutions    

This captures the emotional arc of Narutoâ€™s ninjutsu training:

- clumsy â†’ competent â†’ fluid â†’ transcendent.    

---

# **2. Mastery Structure**

Mastery is tracked both **internally** and **externally**.

### **Internal Mastery (Continuous Value 0â€“100%)**

Used to calculate:

- miscast probability    
- strain reduction    
- stability checks    
- timing windows    
- shortcut unlock thresholds    

### **External Mastery (Tiers)**

Displayed in the journal as:

- Novice    
- Adept    
- Expert    
- Master    

These tiers represent broad plateaus where new abilities unlock.

---

# **3. Glyph Mastery**

Each glyph (hand-sign) has its own mastery path.

### Glyph mastery affects:

- per-glyph strain cost    
- stability when forming the sign    
- visual clarity of the sign    
- chakra flow responsiveness    
- miscast suppression    
- timing generosity    
- subtype interpretation precision    
- feel of executing combos using that glyph    

High glyph mastery = smoother, faster, safer casting.

### Early stage (Novice):

- flickering signs    
- unstable execution    
- distorted visuals    
- small timing window    

### Mid stage (Adept â†’ Expert):

- smoother sign formation    
- lower chakra cost    
- more predictable solo-casts    
- consistent combo integration    

### Late stage (Master):

- crisp, near-perfect sign formation    
- dramatically reduced strain    
- minimal residue on solo-casts    
- signs appear almost automatically    

Glyph mastery is **lifelong** â€” it accumulates across years of play.

---

# **4. Combo Mastery**

Combos also have their own mastery values.

Combo mastery improves:

- rhythm    
- flow-state timing    
- reliability under pressure    
- partial-success quality    
- strain distribution    
- stability of long sequences    

### When a combo reaches high mastery:

- its casting becomes intuitive    
- the ninja requires less conscious effort    
- strain drops significantly    
- timing becomes automatic    
- shortcut glyph potential becomes available    

This models Naruto learning:

- Shadow Clone    
- Rasengan    
- RasenShuriken    
- Big Ball Rasengan    
- Sage variants    

Repetition refines the art.

---

# **5. Unlocking Shortcut Glyphs**

Shortcut glyphs represent **compressed hand-seal sequences**, allowing a long combo to be executed in a fraction of the time.

They are unlocked through a combination of:

### **A) High Glyph Mastery**

Every glyph in the chain must reach high stability.

### **B) High Combo Mastery**

The full combo must be performed many times.

### **C) Bloodline Resonance**

Some lineages naturally accelerate mastery of certain categories and sequences.

When ALL THREE converge, the ninjaâ€™s muscle memory and chakra flow become so refined that:

### **A single shortcut glyph replaces an entire chain.**

Example:

- 5-sign combo â†’ 1 shortcut glyph    
- 5+2-sign combo â†’ 2 shortcut glyphs    

This mirrors the elite-seal-speed of Kakashi, Itachi, or Minato:  
**seemingly instantaneous, but earned through years of discipline.**

---

# **6. Shortcut Glyph Behavior**

Shortcut glyphs:

- appear visually distinct    
- integrate into the playerâ€™s hotbar like normal glyphs    
- are documented in the journal    
- dramatically reduce combo execution time    
- lower strain load    
- increase fluidity in combat    
- are recognized by NPCs (who may react with awe or fear)    

Shortcut glyphs are never gained instantly â€” they emerge only through deep mastery and resonance.

---

# **7. Shortcut Evolution Paths**

Shortcuts are not static.  
They can evolve based on:

### **A) Mastery Evolution**

As mastery deepens, shortcuts become faster, more stable, or more efficient.

### **B) Residue Influence**

Residue-heavy usage may distort shortcuts, creating:

- corrupted variants    
- unstable forms    
- forbidden paths    

### **C) Bloodline Awakening**

Awakened lineages may modify shortcuts:

- new elements    
- enhanced power    
- altered subtype flows    

### **D) World Events**

Anomalies, spiritual calamities, or ancient blessings may alter existing shortcut behavior.

### **E) Usage Patterns**

Repeated exposure to certain biomes or foes shapes shortcuts organically.

This supports long-term character identity and deep replayability.

---

# **8. Mastery Effects on Casting**

Mastery provides the following mechanical benefits:

### **A) Lower Glyph Strain**

Each mastered sign costs less chakra.

### **B) Lower Final Technique Strain**

Long combos become safer.

### **C) Reduced Residue Generation**

Partial successes become cleaner.

### **D) Miscast Suppression**

Stability increases massively.

### **E) Increased Timing Windows**

Casting becomes forgiving.

### **F) Improved Combo Stability**

Long sequences hold together reliably.

### **G) Enhanced Flow State**

Casting feels smooth, fast, intuitive.

This is the essence of the Naruto fantasy:  
**mastery is felt physically and visually, not just as stats.**

---

# **9. Mastery Progression Curve**

Mastery grows according to:

### **D) Training Intensity**

Repeated attempts accelerate mastery.

### **E) Glyph Category Difficulty**

Some signs are simply harder by nature:

- Consume = difficult    
- Veil = easier    
- Flux = volatile    

This means mastery progression is:

- slow early (when chakra is limited)    
- faster mid-game (as discipline grows)    
- fluid late-game (when the ninja becomes an expert)    

The curve is **natural**, not grindy.

---

# **10. Technique Evolutions at Legendary Mastery**

When a combo reaches absolute mastery and resonance, it may evolve.

Evolution conditions include:

- high mastery    
- bloodline awakening    
- residue thresholds    
- long combo length    
- environmental stimuli    

Legendary-level forms include:

### **A) Refined Form**

- cleaner    
- more efficient    
- more powerful    

### **B) Bloodline Variant**

- elements tied to lineage    
- unique behaviors    
- special resonance    

### **C) Forbidden Variant**

- powerful but dangerous    
- world-unique    
- linked to residue    

### **D) Final Form (Long Combo Evolution)**

A 6â€“7 sign combo might gain:

- new branches    
- extended power    
- awakened subtype interactions    
- devastating endgame effects    

This is where the â€œSannin / Kage-levelâ€ jutsu live.

---

# **11. NPC Interaction with Mastery**

NPCs follow the same mastery system:

### Basic Ninja:

- glyph mastery low    
- combo mastery modest    

### Skilled Ninja:

- mixture of mastered glyphs    
- stable standard combos    

### Elite Ninja:

- high mastery across specific glyphs    
- reliable long chains    

### Legendary Ninja:

- shortcut glyphs    
- evolved techniques    
- personalized jutsu forms    
- clan-exclusive evolutions    

This keeps encounters fair and deeply immersive.

NPCs may learn player-invented shortcuts by:

- observing    
- copying    
- defeating the player    
- finding journals after death    
- training together    

---

# â­ **B4 Summary**

The Mastery & Shortcut Glyph system transforms ninjutsu into:

- an evolving art    
- a long-term discipline    
- a lifetime of growth

- a cultural practice

This is where a ninja becomes a legend.

# â­ **B5 â€” HOTBAR INPUT & CASTING SYSTEM (Final, Aligned Edition)**

_How players express ninjutsu through rhythmic glyph input, mobile combat, mastery-driven timing windows, and emergent combo discovery._

---

# **1. Overview**

Sigilborneâ€™s casting system translates **hand-sign ninjutsu** into an intuitive, rhythmic, extremely expressive input model.

This system enables:

- freeform glyph sequencing
- fluid, dynamic combat
- Naruto-style seal-speed mastery
- experimentation and discovery
- player mobility while casting
- shortcut glyphs for instant high-level techniques

Casting is:

- rhythmic, not button-mashy
- intuitive, not UI-heavy
- expressive, not binary
- mastery-driven, not brute-forced

---

# **2. The Recursive Mastery Deck (Hotbar System)**

We accept the constraint: **10 Slots Max**.
This represents the ninja's "active mental focus." You might *know* 50 signs, but you can only keep 10 "at your fingertips" during the chaos of combat.

### **The Deck Building Choice: Primitives vs. Shortcuts**

This creates a natural progression arc for the player:

#### **Novice (The Generalist)**
- **Bar:** `[1:Fire] [2:Wind] [3:Water] [4:Earth] [5:Lightning]` ...
- **Playstyle:** You have all the "letters of the alphabet." You can spell *anything*, but you have to spell it out slowly (`1->2->3`). You are versatile but slow.

#### **Master (The Specialist)**
- **Bar:** `[1:Fireball_Shortcut] [2:MudWall_Shortcut] [3:LightningBlade_Shortcut] [4:Void_Shortcut]` ...
- **Playstyle:** You have replaced the "letters" with "words." You cast complex jutsu instantly.
- **The Cost:** You unmapped the basic `Fire` glyph to make room for `Fireball`. You can no longer cast experimental/random fire combos easily. You have traded **versatility** for **speed and power**.

---

# **3. Recursive Chaining (The Macro System)**

To make this system deep, **Shortcut Glyphs act as valid inputs for NEW combos.**

### **Scenario:**
1. You master `Fire (A)` + `Wind (B)` = `Firestorm (AB)`.
2. You map `AB` to Slot 1.
3. You still have `Earth (C)` on Slot 2.
4. **New Combo Input:** You press `1 (AB)` â†’ `2 (C)`.
5. **Result:** The game interprets this as `A+B+C`.
6. **Effect:** You just cast a 3-sign technique with 2 buttons.

This allows players to build **"Macro-Combos."** You aren't just automating old stuff; you are using the automated stuff as building blocks for *god-tier* jutsu that would be impossible to type out manually in time.

---

# **4. The Tool Belt (Dedicated Utility)**

Tools (Kunai, Smoke Bombs, Potions) do **not** fight for Glyph slots.

**Proposal:**
- **Glyph Bar (1â€“0):** Your magical repertoire (Mental Load).
- **Tool Belt (Q, E, R):** Your physical utility (Muscle Memory).

This separation ensures that using a smoke bomb doesn't require unlearning a spell.

---

# **5. Combo Input Rhythm**

Players cast ninjutsu by pressing hotbar glyph keys in a rhythm:

```
1 â†’ 4 â†’ 2 â†’ 5 â†’ â€¦
```

Each keypress:

- adds a glyph to the chain
- emits a symbolic particle flash
- plays a subtle sound cue
- begins or continues the â€œcombo timing windowâ€

There are no invalid inputs â€” every sequence is an _attempt_.

---

# **6. Dynamic Timing Window (Mastery-Based)**

Ninjutsu is cast using a **timing window** that grows with mastery.

### **Novice**

- small window
- nervous, shaky casting
- combos often cut short

### **Adept**

- moderate window
- manageable rhythm
- early flow feeling

### **Expert**

- large window
- long combos are stable
- rhythm becomes intuitive

### **Master**

- very large window
- almost no accidental combo cuts
- long chains flow like choreography

### **Shortcut Glyphs**

- near-instant execution
- timing window irrelevant
- still rhythmic for chaining combos

This system imitates Narutoâ€™s seal-speed progression exactly.

---

# **7. The H1 Combo Resolution Model (Canonical)**

This is the core of Sigilborneâ€™s input philosophy.

When the timing window expires, the game resolves the sequence using this priority order:

---

## **1. If sequence = known / mastered combo**

âž¡ **Full technique**  
Stable, powerful, predictable.

---

## **2. If sequence = partially mastered combo**

âž¡ **Partial technique**  
Weaker or incomplete:

- shaky clone
- flickering veil
- weak projectile
- unstable elemental pulse

---

## **3. If sequence = PLAUSIBLE but new**

âž¡ **Experimental technique**  
A low-power, unstable effect that hints at a potential new combo.

Examples:

- small puff of bloom
- faint distortion
- weak shockwave
- half-formed barrier

This is the **player-invented jutsu path**.

---

## **4. If sequence ends with ONE glyph and no follow-up**

âž¡ **Solo-cast the final glyph**  
Used for:

- probing
- testing glyph effects
- low-risk tactical plays
- mastery training

Solo-casts never happen by accident â€” they require intentional delay.

---

## **5. If sequence = true nonsense (invalid category flow)**

âž¡ **Fizzle + minor strain**  
Chakra disrupts and dissipates.

Fizzle effects:

- small spark
- puff of disrupted energy
- brief aura flicker

Never punishing. Always readable.

---

# **8. Interruptibility**

Casting _can_ be interrupted, but the rules are dynamic:

### **Novice**

- easily interrupted
- even small hits break focus
- lost confidence

### **Adept**

- less interrupted by small damage
- movement still affects stability

### **Expert**

- can weave seals while moving or dodging
- minor hits barely affect rhythm

### **Master**

- extremely difficult to interrupt
- only elite NPCs or heavy attacks disrupt them

### **Combo Length Matters**

- long chains = more interruptible
- shortcut glyphs = rare windows of vulnerability

This simulates true shinobi duels.

---

# **9. Mobility While Casting**

Mobility is not fixed â€” itâ€™s a function of skill, mastery, and technique type.

### **Novice**

- movement easily breaks focus
- safer to stand still

### **Adept**

- can walk while forming short sequences
- long sequences require more care

### **Expert**

- can run while forming seals
- mid-combat casting becomes viable

### **Master**

- fully mobile
- seal weaving while sprinting or dodging
- shortcut glyphs feel instantaneous

### **Technique Restrictions**

Some techniques inherently require stillness, e.g.:

- spatial flux
- illusion weaves
- large-scale bloom transformations

---

# **10. Casting Feedback (Minimalistic & Diegetic)**

Sigilborne uses **clean, stylized, symbolic feedback**:

### âœ” Symbolic Glyph Particles

Small sigils flash near the hands.

### âœ” Subtle Sound Cues

Soft chimes / whispers indicate successful input.

### âŒ No UI progress bar.

No clutter. No MMO-style casting bars.

This keeps everything grounded, diegetic, and readable in top-down 2D.

---

# **11. Mistakes During Casting**

There are **no wrong inputs**.

If a player hits an unexpected glyph:

- it is simply added to the sequence
- the interpretation model evaluates the entire chain
- players may accidentally discover new jutsu
- nothing is invalid or â€œbrokenâ€

This preserves:

- creative freedom
- emergent techniques
- non-linear discovery
- ninja intuition fantasy

---

# **12. Holding & Sustain**

Sigilborne distinguishes between **input** and **technique sustain**.

### **Input**

- glyphs are always TAP-based
- no holding during combo formation

### **Sustain**

Some categories allow maintaining an effect after casting:

- **Pulse** â†’ beams, sustained force
- **Veil** â†’ maintained invisibility or distortion
- **Flux** â†’ transformation states
- **Project** â†’ continuous streams

Sustain drains chakra or increases strain depending on mastery.

---

# **13. Shortcut Glyph Casting (Recursive)**

Shortcut glyphs:

- cast nearly instantly
- replace long chains
- preserve rhythm for chaining
- reduce strain
- increase mobility
- still respect mastery
- still interruptible by elite enemies

Shortcut casting becomes central to late-game combat flow.

---

# **14. Accessibility (Current Phase)**

For now:

- no assist modes
- no slowed timing
- no special accessibility toggles

These may be introduced later without modifying core mechanics.

---

# **15. Stylized 2D Sign Representation**

In Sigilborne:

- no hand animations
- no 3D rigging
- no complex finger tracking

Instead:

- stylized 2D sigils
- particle-based glyph effects
- arcane strokes
- subtle flare patterns

This gives:

- clean readability
- fast input feedback
- consistent martial-arts energy
- strong visual identity

Perfect for top-down 2D.

---

# â­ **B5 Summary**

The Hotbar Input & Casting System provides:

- rhythmic, expressive ninjutsu
- dynamic mastery-driven timing
- freeform combo experimentation
- graceful mistake handling
- fully mobile casting at high mastery
- instant seal-speed via shortcut glyphs
- clean, diegetic feedback
- no UI clutter
- deep tactical expression
- infinite technique discovery

Itâ€™s the perfect mechanical expression of your ninja-life simulator vision.

# â­ **B6 â€” Bloodlines (Alignment Questions First)**
_Procedural mystical lineages that shape identity, mastery, power, danger, and the long arc of a ninjaâ€™s life._

---

# **1. Overview**

Bloodlines in Sigilborne are **procedurally generated, world-specific, mutable geneticâ€“mystical lineages** that influence:

- chakra growth
- casting quirks
- mastery acceleration
- unique abilities
- hidden awakenings
- clan identity
- relationships
- forbidden mutations
- technique evolution
- NPC reactions
- world politics

Every world produces its own **unique set of bloodlines**, with:

- unique names
- unique visual traits
- unique affinities
- unique awakening triggers
- unique evolutions
- unique weaknesses
- unique power ceilings

No bloodline ever appears twice across different worlds.  
Each playthrough is a new universe of lineage possibilities.

---

# **2. Procedural Rarity Model**

Bloodline rarity is dynamic and world-dependent.

### Bloodline frequency varies by:

- **world seed**
- **region**
- **historical clan structure**
- **past calamities**
- **ancestral events**
- **residue density**

In some worlds:

- bloodlines may be nearly extinct
- only one or two people possess them

In others:

- bloodline clans flourish
- many NPCs possess lesser variants

This system ensures:

- infinite replayability
- distinct world identities
- wildly different political landscapes

---

# **3. Bloodline Generation Templates**

Each bloodline is generated from a **template class**, which defines its general shape but not its details.

Examples of template classes:

- **Sensory Lineages** (perception, vision, awareness)
- **Force Lineages** (chakra output, physical boosts)
- **Mind Lineages** (illusions, mental resistance)
- **Resonance Lineages** (affinity to anomalies or spirits)
- **Corruption Lineages** (tainted origins, high-risk evolution)
- **Inherited Beasts** (tailed-beast-like spiritual entities)
- **Ancient Seal Bearers** (linked to old glyph sequences)
- **Body Morphic Lineages** (exoforms, transformations)

Each template contains rules for generating:

- powers
- weaknesses
- awakenings
- evolutions
- mutations

But the **actual content** is entirely procedural.

This mirrors:

- Sharingan-type templates
- Byakugan-type templates
- tailed-beast templates
- kekkei genkai variants
- etc.

Without copying anything directly.

---

# **4. Bloodline Traits & Mechanical Effects**

Bloodlines may influence _every system_ in Sigilborne.

Final confirmed list:

### âœ” A) Easier mastery of specific glyph categories

A sensory bloodline might heavily boost Veil & Echo.  
A physical lineage might boost Bloom & Surge.

### âœ” B) Adjusted chakra growth rate

Some grow chakra faster.  
Some slower.  
Some have high peak but low regen.  
Some fluctuate.

### âœ” C) Passive traits

Sharper senses  
Faster healing  
Reduced fatigue  
Enhanced mobility  
Pain resistance  
Residual awareness

### âœ” D) Active ability unlocks

Signature jutsu  
Innate transformations  
Clairvoyance bursts  
Resonance detection

### âœ” E) Signature bloodline techniques

World-unique abilities that only this bloodline can awaken.

### âœ” F) Modified residue behavior

Some lineages resist corruption.  
Some attract it.  
Some transform through it.  
Some thrive under it.

### âœ” G) Unique casting quirks

Distinct finger movements  
Altered sign glow  
Different timing feel  
Different category synergy

### âœ” H) Weaknesses / curses

Chakra instability  
Anomaly vulnerability  
Mental fragility  
Loss of control under strain  
Shortened lifespan

### âœ” I) Clan teaching access

Clans only teach their heritage techniques to their kind.  
Others view outsiders with suspicion.

### âœ” J) Anomaly resistance / vulnerability

Spirit resonance  
Flux perception  
Illusion resistance  
Spatial instability

---

# **5. Bloodline Mutation Model**

Sigilborne uses a **hybrid mutation model**:

### **Per World:**

Bloodlines are ALWAYS different:

- new name
- new visual traits
- new inner logic
- new powers and weaknesses
- new rarity
- new awakenings

### **Per Generation:**

Within the same world, bloodlines can mutate:

- slightly (normal)
- moderately (when exposed to residue)
- drastically (rare events, clan tragedies, forbidden arts)

### **Per Character:**

Bloodlines may diverge based on:

- training
- trauma
- corruption
- personal choices
- interaction with anomalies
- mastery of forbidden techniques

This creates a storyline where:

- bloodlines survive
- evolve
- fracture
- go extinct
- reemerge
- become legends
- become curses

All organically.

---

# **6. Bloodline Awakening System**

Bloodlines NEVER start fully active.

A bloodline may awaken through:

### **D) Emotional/traumatic events**

Loss, fear, near-death, extreme stress.

### **E) Residue exposure**

Direct contact with corrupted zones.  
Overuse of unstable combos.  
Forbidden experiments.

### **F) World events**

Spirit surges  
Anomaly eruptions  
Leyline ruptures  
Clan-level rituals

These awakenings:

- alter appearance
- unlock abilities
- shift aura
- modify mastery rates
- change how NPCs perceive the player

Awakening is always a **big moment** â€” a rite of passage.

---

# **7. Clan Integration Model**

Most bloodlines belong to clans, but not all.

### âœ” B) Mixed model with rare isolated bloodlines

- Some bloodlines form multi-generational clans
- Some appear only once: a unique child in the world
- Some clans split into factions
- Some bloodlines die out mid-playthrough
- Some strengthen as NPCs train them

Unique bloodline characters can become:

- allies
- rivals
- bosses

# **2. Static Category Resonance (Universal Across All Worlds)**

These relationships NEVER change, ensuring a consistent â€œmagic physicsâ€ foundation.

### âœ” **Bloom**

> Strong in: forests, fertile fields, swamps, jungles

### âœ” **Veil**

### âœ” **Echo**

### âœ” **Flux**

### âœ” **Surge**

### âœ” **Consume**

**These pairings never change across playthroughs.**

# **1. Overview**

Combat in Sigilborne is built on four pillars:

1. **Speed** â€” fast, reactive, high-pressure encounters
2. **Lethality** â€” mistakes can kill, depending on the enemy
3. **Mastery** â€” skill, timing, and focus matter more than stats
4. **Symmetry** â€” NPCs follow the same casting and movement rules as players

The game is not:

- Souls-like slow
- button-mashing
- locked animation combat
- or MMO cooldown spam

Itâ€™s systemic ninja combat where:

- movement
- timing

- environmental resonance
- mastery differences
- and enemy intelligence

all combine into emergent battles.

---

# **2. Combat Pace**

Combat is **fast, high-pressure, and reactive**.

- enemies strike with intent

- combos must be executed under tension
- dodging and chakra movement are key survival tools

The pace is comparable to:

- early-to-mid Naruto
- Sekiroâ€™s tempo (not its parry dependence)

# **3. Lethality & Danger Gradient**

### Weak opponents

- predictable
- limited threat
- low lethality

### Trained ninja

- punishing
- can interrupt casting
- force movement
- can kill in 2â€“3 mistakes

### Elite ninja

### Legendary/Jonin-tier

- terrifying

- hard counters
- can one-shot the player

Danger is **situational**, not fixed.

# **7. Interruptibility (Core Rule)**

### âœ” **Every non-instant technique is interruptible.**

This is universal and predictable.

- being struck breaks sequences
- being staggered breaks sequences
- being thrown off-balance increases miscast chance

Instant glyphs (single-sign techniques) are not interruptible  
but still suffer movement-related instability.

---

# **8. Casting Mobility (Canonical Rule)**

This is your final chosen design:

### âœ” All techniques are fully mobile.

You can always move while weaving signs.

### âœ” Movement reduces focus

Penalty increases:

- miscast risk
- strain
- timing errors
- instability
- residue generation

### âœ” Mastery reduces the movement penalty

Elite casters can:

- sprint
- dash
- dodge
- glide mid-air  
    while maintaining sign sequences with only minor risk.

### âœ” No technique ever hard-locks movement

There is no rooting, channeling, or forced stillness.

Movement is always in the playerâ€™s control.

---

# **9. Casting Under Pressure (Mastery-Driven)**

Early-game:

- standing still is safest
- moving while casting is risky
- low-tier enemies break casting easily

- mobility windows extend
- timing becomes intuitive

# **1. Overview**

# **2. Stealth Progression Curve**

Stealth is **weak early**, **viable mid-game**, and **powerful at high mastery**, but always counterable.

### Early Game

- noise control is bad
- chakra leaks constantly
- enemies detect easily
- basic ambush possible against weak foes only

### Mid Game

- stable chakra signature
- learned movement discipline
- stealth takedowns viable
- re-stealth possible with skill and timing
- environmental stealth becomes reliable

### Late Game (High Stealth Mastery)

- advanced Veil/Echo techniques
- nearly invisible in resonant environments
- silent movement
- delayed detection windows
- mid-fight stealth transitions
- high-risk assassination builds become playable

### Mastery Rule:

**Stealth only improves if the player trains stealth, not via generic combat.**

Training options:

- Veil drills
- Echo discipline training
- resonance concealment practice
- environmental stealth training
- mentor-based stealth lessons
- infiltration missions

---

# **3. Types of Stealth**

Sigilborne supports three stealth modes:

### **1. Physical Stealth (no chakra)**

- pure silence
- hiding in shadows
- minimizing sound
- line-of-sight management
- camouflage using terrain

### **2. Chakra Stealth (Veil/Echo techniques)**

- chakra signature damping
- shadow blending
- aura suppression
- vibration masking
- resonance cloaking

Costs chakra but far more powerful.

### **3. Corrupted Stealth (Consume/Flux hybrid)**

- chaotic signature scrambling
- chakra distortion aura
- anti-sensing fields
- unpredictable detection behavior

High-risk, high-reward, residue-dependent.

### **1. Sight**

- vision cones
- light sensitivity

### **2. Sound**

- footsteps
- clothing friction
- rustling foliage

### **3. Chakra Sensing**

### **4. Resonance Awareness**

- sand (Gaara-style)

- bloodline traits
- residue levels

### Dumb enemies

### Bloom Techniques

- environmental camouflage

### Consume Techniques

This is your confirmed design.

# **1. Overview**

- notice residue
- interpret resonance fields
- anticipate attacks
- counter stealth
- navigate anomalies

- **mastery-dependent** (range, clarity, fidelity improve)
- **enemy-type dependent**
- **resonance-dependent**
- **bloodline-dependent**
- **corruption-dependent**

No one has omniscient perception.

Chakra sensing is not universal â€” but itâ€™s not rare either.

### Tier 4 â€” Long Range

### Tier 5 â€” Battlefield Range

Range is meaningful, balanced by strain and chakra cost.

_Environmental discipline without tedious survival-game mechanics._

---

# **1. Overview**

Sigilborne is **not** a survival game.  
There is:

- **no hunger meter**
- **no thirst**
- **no hunting system**
- **no temperature damage**
- **no survival crafting**

Instead, survival is about **ninja discipline**, **environmental pressure**, and **maintaining your chakra**, not micromanaging basic needs.

Survival is expressed through:

- fatigue
- stamina
- sleep
- meditation
- weather
- resonance
- sickness and poison
- environmental hazards
- long missions
- stealth conditions

This creates immersion and danger **without ever becoming a chore**.

---

# **2. Core Survival Philosophy**

### âœ” Survival is **secondary**, never the main loop

### âœ” It matters in long missions, hostile climates, and stealth

### âœ” It supports ninja fantasy, not distracts from it

### âœ” It creates tension, not annoyance

You donâ€™t play _against_ survival.  
You play _through_ the environment as a ninja.

---

# **3. No Hunger or Thirst (Your Choice)**

There is **zero hunger or thirst system**.

- No meters.
- No penalties for not eating.
- No foraging or hunting loops.

Food exists only for:

- buffs
- romance / dates
- rare rituals
- comfort/flavor

This keeps the focus on mastery, stealth, and combat.

---

# **4. Sleep & Fatigue (Strong System)**

Sleep is **required** to restore:

- chakra stability
- focus
- strain tolerance
- pain threshold
- sensing clarity

### Fatigue impacts:

- casting precision
- stealth noise
- movement recovery
- reaction time
- pain resistance

### Lack of sleep (overexertion) causes:

- elevated strain
- miscast risk
- unstable chakra flow
- hallucination-like perception distortions
- poor stealth
- poor sensing

Fatigue is **dangerous**, but **not lethal**.

---

# **5. Meditation (Partial Recovery)**

Meditation restores:

- some chakra
- some focus
- mild fatigue relief

But:

- it does NOT replace sleep
- long missions without real rest are risky
- meditation becomes extremely effective with mastery

This aligns with ninja discipline.

---

# **6. Food & Cooking (Buff System Only)**

Cooking exists **entirely for buffs**, not survival.

Buff examples:

- improved chakra regen
- emotional boost for training
- increased focus window
- enhanced stealth duration
- date scenes and social bonding

No survival dependency.  
Eating is **optional** but strategically useful.

---

# **7. Weather Effects (Strong System)**

Weather alters gameplay but does not kill.

### Weather impacts:

- visibility
- stealth difficulty
- chakra stability
- movement
- ranged weapons
- residue spread
- sensing accuracy

### Examples:

- rain disrupts Echo (vibration) sensing
- heavy fog buffs Veil stealth
- strong winds weaken projectile accuracy
- dry desert heat increases fatigue
- cold climates slow chakra circulation

But **none of these cause direct HP damage**.

---

# **8. Temperature (Fatigue-Only Model)**

Extreme heat/cold affects:

- fatigue rate
- chakra stability
- mobility
- stealth difficulty

But **never causes health damage or death**.

This avoids annoying survival loops while keeping immersion strong.

---

# **9. Resonance-Based Environment Effects (Strong Integration)**

Every environment has a resonance alignment:

- **Veil zones** â†’ buff stealth, weaken loud movement
- **Echo zones** â†’ amplify sound, hinder stealth
- **Bloom zones** â†’ boost healing, hinder certain illusions
- **Consume zones** â†’ scramble sensing, buff corrupted builds
- **Flux zones** â†’ unpredictable danger, aura distortions

This integrates perfectly with B7 (Resonance), B9 (Combat), B10 (Stealth), and B11 (Sensing).

---

# **10. Environmental Stealth (Strong Impact)**

Stealth is deeply influenced by the environment:

- mist
- shadows
- foliage
- storm noise
- caves
- crowded areas
- night vs day

Weather + resonance + terrain together define stealth difficulty.

This keeps stealth strategic and realistic.

---

# **11. Sickness, Poison & Disease (A â€” Dangerous, Realistic)**

While survival needs are light, **illness and poison matter a lot**.

Sources:

- tainted food
- residue corruption
- poison tags
- venomous creatures
- environmental spores
- certain jutsu
- corrupted water sources

Effects include:

- chakra instability
- hallucination-like symptoms
- decreased sensing
- reduced movement
- pain spikes

This is a major part of ninja realism.

---

# **12. Mental Fatigue (Strong System)**

Separate from physical fatigue:

- long missions
- trauma
- sleeplessness
- chakra overuse
- emotional events

Mental fatigue affects:

- sensing
- glyph precision
- combo timing
- perception
- illusion resistance

This creates depth without micromanagement.

---

# **13. Procedural Weather & Climate (A)**

Each world has:

- seasons
- climates
- weather patterns
- anomalies
- spiritual storms
- regional hazards

This makes each world feel alive and unique.

---

# **14. Clan Survival Specialties (Your Choice: No)**

Clans do **not** have special survival bonuses like â€œdesert clan = heat resistance.â€

This keeps survival simple and non-intrusive.

---

# **15. No Survival Crafting (C)**

No crafting of tents, shelters, clothing, etc.

### Survival is based on:

- discipline
- rest
- meditation
- weather-readiness
- ninja tools
- environmental wisdom

Not crafting campfires.

---

# **16. Environmental Danger (B â€” Non-Lethal)**

Cold wonâ€™t kill you.  
Heat wonâ€™t kill you.  
Storms wonâ€™t kill you.

### Environment impacts _performance_, not life.

This avoids survival annoyances while keeping strategy.

---

# â­ **B14 Summary**

Sigilborneâ€™s survival system is:

- NOT a traditional survival game
- fatigue & sleep matter
- meditation helps but doesnâ€™t replace sleep
- weather strongly affects gameplay
- resonance ties to environment
- stealth deeply tied to terrain & weather
- food is for buffs/social, not survival
- poison & sickness add danger
- extreme environments influence fatigue, not HP
- no hunger
- no thirst
- no crafting of survival gear
- survival = ninja discipline, not meters

This is the correct level of depth for a ninja RPG.

---

# â­ **B15 â€” ANIMALS, SPIRITS, CREATURES & FAUNA (Alignment Questions Next)**
_A living ecological framework where natural wildlife, spiritual entities, corrupt anomalies, and mythical beings coexist inside a procedurally generated ninja world._

---

# **1. Overview**

Sigilborneâ€™s world is alive â€” biologically, spiritually, and metaphysically.

This includes:

- natural fauna
- spirit creatures

- resonance-aligned creatures
- mythical titans
- procedural species
- reactive ecological behaviors

This system integrates directly with:

- B7 (Resonance)
- B10 (Stealth)
- B11 (Sensing)
- B12 (Damage/Trauma)
- world generation (B1/B2)

The goal: a world that _feels alive_, unpredictable, and full of ancient and emergent life.

- deer
- boar

- birds
- insects
- fish

- prey

They behave realistically and respond to:

- noise
- movement

- scent
- weather
- resonance events

Animals react to ninja behavior:

- flee when spooked

- reveal your location
- attack if cornered
- detect inexperienced stealth
- ignore high-mastery stealth

Some animals are natural â€œdanger detectors,â€ especially:

- birds
- dogs/wolf-like species
- spirit-attuned beasts

# **4. Aggression (A)**

Species vary naturally:

- predators â†’ aggressive under conditions
- prey â†’ flee
- corrupted â†’ hostile
- territorial animals â†’ attack if threatened
- nocturnal hunters â†’ stalk

No cheap aggro behavior â€” all aggression is ecological.

# **5. Resource Drops (A)**

Animals yield materials for:

- rituals
- medicine
- poison creation

- spiritual offerings
- seal inks

But **no survival necessity** (consistent with B14).

# **6. Spirit Creatures (A â€” Full Ecosystem)**

### Types include:

Visible only in **resonance zones** (C)

### **Mid-Tier Spirits**

Visible only to **trained sensors** (B)

Visible only through:

- rituals
- special items

Spirits respond differently depending on their nature:

- Bloom spirits â†’ strong in forests, healing areas
- Veil spirits â†’ thrive in shadows, illusions
- Echo spirits â†’ best in caves, stone regions
- Surge spirits â†’ storm affinity
- Flux spirits â†’ anomaly-born
- Consume spirits â†’ tied to death, decay, corruption

Not all spirits follow the same pattern â€” some break rules.

---

# **10. Corrupted Creatures (Residue) (A)**

Residue corrupts:

- animals â†’ twisted forms

- weak but persistent  
    to
- elite â€œboss-levelâ€ corrupted beasts

- plague wolves
- residue leeches
- flux titans
- corrupted insects

This prevents the world from collapsing uncontrollably.

This makes stealth fresh and unpredictable.

Creatures react strongly to:

This makes the world feel ancient and alive.

# **20. Procedural Species Variability (A)**

# â­ **B15 Summary**
